posted:Posted November 5, 2023
msg:The location of this hotel is not superior. It is located in Jiangning University Town, about a 40-minute drive from the city center. There is no business within one kilometer of the surrounding area. But it is only a few steps away from Fangshan Scenic Area. The hotel is a mid-range brand owned by MGM. The hotel has a total of four floors, and the architectural form encloses several courtyards of different sizes. The underground floor is for the garage and fitness center, and the first floor is for conferences and restaurants. The style of this hotel is more business-like. The overall design of the hotel is modern and simple, and the stainless steel lion sculpture at the main entrance is very recognizable. Abandoning the complex decoration of traditional five-star hotels. The indoor space in the public part is simple and elegant, and the corridors of the guest rooms are carpeted, making it relatively quiet. The basic room types of guest rooms have ample space. The balcony room faces a green space next to it. It is very quiet. The birds chirping in the morning give it a very ecological feel. The design of the guest rooms is also relatively restrained, and the materials used are relatively simple. There is no traditional writing desk, but a small round table instead, which is more convenient for working, drinking tea, and dining. The bathroom in the guest room is from Kohler brand, and the toiletries are from Karl Lagerfeld, which is quite good. The gym is fully equipped. The hotel's breakfast doesn't have many varieties, but it has local characteristics. The Lao Ya vermicelli soup, pot stickers, and steamed pastries all taste good. The hotel welcome, front desk and room service are still very prompt, and the sanitary conditions are also good. The waiters in the design restaurant are relatively young and the quality of service needs to be improved. In short, this is a pretty good business hotel, but the configuration inside (lawn canopy, swimming pool, first-floor guest room courtyard) can accommodate family travel. The hotel strikes a good balance between five-star hotel luxury and price. If your activity range is near Jiangning University Town, I highly recommend it.
